posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:The room is pretty good. Unlike the regular rooms, which have a long and narrow corridor at the entrance, the door is closer to the bed. I was a little uncomfortable at first, but the bed is really big. After placing the stool at the end of the bed, it is still kept at a certain distance from the TV, which shows that the room is not small. The service is especially good. I missed her Tremella soup in the evening on the first day of leaving. It was very sticky and the sweetness was just right. I brought my baby to check in, and the little brother also gave the baby a puppy doll, which was very happy. There are some shortcomings. First, the room facilities are not up to date. For example, the bedspread under the mattress is still tattered and has not been replaced. The small shower nozzle has many holes blocked, so only the big nozzle can be used. Second, the cleaning auntie didn't seem to know whether the room was extended. After cleaning the room, she didn't replenish the mineral water in time, but the auntie was very enthusiastic. After we informed the front desk, she immediately sent four bottles and asked if it was enough. Especially at night, she would take the initiative to ask if Tremella soup was needed. Finally, the breakfast soup is really good, which is highly praised. In short, it is super cost-effective to stay at this price during May Day. I highly recommend it. The only pity is that I forgot to take pictures with my baby
